/// Logic
class Main
{
    MaxTitans = 50;
    TitanSpawnRate = 50;
    TimeLimit = 1200;

    TimeLimitTooltip = "In seconds. Set to 0 if you don't want time limit.";
    TitanSpawnRateTooltip = "A value between 0 and 100. Higher means titans will spawn faster";

    _DefenseOnly = false; # For Debugging. Skips HQ part, also causes some issues with MP

    /* 
     * Once titans' capture progress of the HQ is over
     * this value, the game will show a warning dialogue for the human players.
     * Dialogue won't always be shown once the capture progress is exactly this value,
     * instead it will randomly decides whether to show it or not. If it decided to not show,
     * it will wait for a few seconds before trying it again until its shown at least once.
     */
    _ShowWarningDialogueProgress = 0.5;
    _ShowWarningDialogueRetryTime = 10;
    
    _dialogueWasShown = false;
    _currentRetryTime = 0;
    _lastCaptureProgress = 0;

    _difficulty = 0;

    function OnGameStart()
    {
        SupplyAndTpZones.Setup();
        SupplyAndTpZones.SetEnabled(false);
        
        CaptureZones.Setup(self);
        CaptureZones.SetActiveCaptureZones(false);

        self._difficulty = Game.GetGeneralSetting("Difficulty");

        if (Network.IsMasterClient)
        {
            endlessRespawnEnabled = Game.GetMiscSetting("EndlessRespawnEnabled");
            if (!endlessRespawnEnabled)
            {
                key = Input.GetKeyName("General/Pause");
                help = "(Press <b>" + key + "</b> → Game → Misc → Endless respawn)";
                error = "<b><color=#faedcd>[Info]: </color></b>";
                str = "Enabling endless respawn is recommended while playing this mode. ";
                str += "To enable it go to the game setting and under the Misc tab, check the 'Endless respawn' option. ";
                Game.Print(error + str + String.Newline + help);
            }

            TitanSpawnPoints.Setup();
            
            Titans.Setup(self.MaxTitans, self.TitanSpawnRate);
            GameState.TimeLimit = self.TimeLimit;

            GameState.Setup(self._difficulty);
            GameState.Start(self._DefenseOnly);
        }
    }

    function OnCaptured(captureZone, newOwner)
    {
        if (Network.IsMasterClient == false)
        {
            return;
        }

        if (newOwner == "Human" || newOwner == "Titan")
        {
            if (captureZone == CaptureZones.HeadquarterZone && newOwner == "Titan")
            {
                Dialogues.ShowDialogue("LoseByCapture", 1, 2);
                GameState.End(false);
                return;
            }

            if (Titans.CheckForWin())
            {
                Dialogues.ShowDialogue("Win", 2, 2);
                GameState.End(true);
                return;
            }
        }
    }

    function OnNetworkMessage(sender, message)
    {
        data = Json.LoadFromString(message);
        type = data.Get("Type");
        if (type == "Sync")
        {
            syncType = data.Get("SyncType");
            if (syncType == "GameState")
            {
                GameState.DefendStarted = data.Get("DefendStarted");
                if (GameState.DefendStarted)
                {
                    CaptureZones.SetActiveCaptureZones(true);
                    SupplyAndTpZones.SetEnabled(true);
                }
            }
        }
        elif (type == "Dialogue")
        {
            key = data.Get("Key");
            profileIndex = data.Get("ProfileIndex");
            delay = data.Get("Delay");
            Dialogues._ShowDialogueDelayed(key, profileIndex, delay);
        }
        elif (type == "InfoMessage")
        {
            msgType = data.Get("MsgType");
            if (msgType == "SpecialNotAllowed")
            {
                Game.Print("<b>Supply</b> and <b>Shifter</b> specials are not allowed");
            }
            elif (msgType == "PlayerTitansNotAllowed")
            {
                Game.Print("Player <b>Titans</b> and <b>Shifters</b> are not allowed");
            }
        }
        else
        {
            # Game.Print(message);
        }
    }

    coroutine OnPlayerJoin(player)
    {
        if (Network.IsMasterClient)
        {
            wait 0.3;
            NetworkMessage()
                .Set("Type", "Sync")
                .Set("SyncType", "GameState")
                .Set("DefendStarted", GameState.DefendStarted)
                .Send(player);
        }
    }

    coroutine OnPlayerSpawn(player, character)
    {
        if (Network.IsMasterClient == false)
        {
            return;
        }

        if (character != null)
        {
            if (character.Type == "Human")
            {
                wait 0.3;
                s = character.CurrentSpecial;
                if (s == "Supply" || s == "Eren" || s == "Annie" || s == "Armored")
                {
                    character.SetSpecial("Potato");
                    NetworkMessage()
                        .Set("Type", "InfoMessage")
                        .Set("MsgType", "SpecialNotAllowed")
                        .Send(player);
                }
                if (!self._DefenseOnly && !GameState.DefendStarted)
                {
                    character.CurrentGas = 0.0;
                    if (self._difficulty == 0)
                    {
                        character.CurrentGas = 50.0;
                    }
                    elif (self._difficulty == 1)
                    {
                        character.CurrentGas = 10.0;
                    }
                }
            }
            elif (character.Type == "Titan" || character.Type == "Shifter")
            {
                wait 0.3;
                character.GetKilled("Server");
                NetworkMessage()
                        .Set("Type", "InfoMessage")
                        .Set("MsgType", "PlayerTitansNotAllowed")
                        .Send(player);
            }
        }
    }

    function OnCharacterDie(victim, killer, killerName)
    {
        if (Network.IsMasterClient == false)
        {
            return;
        }

        if (victim != null && victim.Type == "Titan" && killer != null)
        {
            Titans.RemoveTitan(victim);
        }
    }

    function OnTick()
    {
        if (Network.IsMasterClient == false)
        {
            return;
        }

        Titans.Update();
    }

    function OnSecond()
    {
        if (Network.IsMasterClient == false)
        {
            return;
        }

        GameState.UpdateRoundTime();

        progress = CaptureZones.HeadquarterZone.GetCaptureProgress();
        if (progress > self._lastCaptureProgress)
        {
            if (progress >= self._ShowWarningDialogueProgress && !self._dialogueWasShown)
            {
                if (self._currentRetryTime <= 0)
                {
                    self._dialogueWasShown = Random.RandomFloat(0, 1) > 0.65;
                    if (!self._dialogueWasShown)
                    {
                        self._currentRetryTime = self._currentRetryTime;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        Dialogues.ShowDialogue("Captured50", 1, 2);
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    self._currentRetryTime -= 1;
                }
            }
        }
        else
        {
            self._dialogueWasShown = false;
        }

        self._lastCaptureProgress = progress;
    }
}
extension GameState
{
    Ended = false;
    DefendStarted = false;

    TimeLimit = 1200;
    CurrentTime = 0;
    TimeLimitEnabled = true;

    Difficulty = 0;

    function Setup(difficulty)
    {
        self.Difficulty = difficulty;
        self.CurrentTime = self.TimeLimit;
        self.TimeLimitEnabled = self.TimeLimit >= 15;
    }

    function Start(skipHeadquarters)
    {
        if (!skipHeadquarters)
        {
            Titans.SpawnHeadquarterTitans();
            self.ShowDialogueStartHQ();
        }
        else
        {
            GameState.StartDefendPhase();
        }
    }

    coroutine ShowDialogueStartHQ()
    {
        wait 4.0;
        Dialogues.ShowDialogue("StartHQ", 0, 0);
    }

    coroutine StartDefendPhase()
    {
        self.DefendStarted = true;
        Titans.StartSpawn();
        NetworkMessage()
            .Set("Type", "Sync")
            .Set("SyncType", "GameState")
            .Set("DefendStarted", self.DefendStarted)
            .SendAll();

        wait 4.0;
        Dialogues.ShowDialogue("EndHQ", 1, 0);
    }

    function UpdateRoundTime()
    {
        if (Network.IsMasterClient == false || self.TimeLimitEnabled == false)
        {
            return;
        }

        self.CurrentTime -= 1;
        if (self.CurrentTime <= 0)
        {
            Dialogues.ShowDialogue("LoseByTimeout", 1, 2);
            self.CurrentTime = 0;
            self.End(false);
        }

        InGameUI.UpdateRoundTime(self.CurrentTime);
    }

    function End(win)
    {
        if (self.Ended) 
        {
            return;
        }

        if (win)
        {
            UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "Humanity wins!");
        }
        else
        {
            UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "Humanity failed!");
        }

        Game.End(10);
        self.Ended = true;
    }
}
extension Dialogues
{
    _locale = Dict();
    _profiles = List();

    function Init()
    {
        englishTexts = Dict();
        englishTexts.Set("Armin", "Armin");
        englishTexts.Set("Jean", "Jean");
        englishTexts.Set("Pixis", "Pixis");

        englishTexts.Set("StartHQ", "We must clear the headquarters of titans before we can refill our gas supplies! Fight with all you've got!");
        englishTexts.Set("EndHQ", "Headquarters is secure! Refill your gas and prepare to take back the city!");
        englishTexts.Set("Captured50", "We're losing control of the headquarters! Defend it at all costs!");
        englishTexts.Set("LoseByCapture", "We've lost the headquarters! Fall back and regroup!");
        englishTexts.Set("LoseByTimeout", "We couldn't recapture the city in time. The titans remain a threat.");
        englishTexts.Set("Win", "We've reclaimed the city! Great work soldiers, humanity wins this day!");

        chineseTexts = Dict();
        chineseTexts.Set("Armin", "阿尔敏");
        chineseTexts.Set("Jean", "让");
        chineseTexts.Set("Pixis", "多托·匹西斯司令");

        chineseTexts.Set("StartHQ", "各位，我们需要清除掉室内巨人才能安全补给");
        chineseTexts.Set("EndHQ", "太好了，有了气体补给我们就可以出去杀了这些巨人，但是不要忘了保护中心补给点");
        chineseTexts.Set("Captured50", "喂喂喂，怎么回事！中心补给站要失守了，快回去清理掉区域内巨人");
        chineseTexts.Set("LoseByCapture", "可恶，明明守住补给点就能夺回城市！明天我就要去内地当大爷了，为什么？");
        chineseTexts.Set("LoseByTimeout", "罢了，老夫顶多再添败绩一次，但是战线太久，士兵损耗严重，全员撤退！");
        chineseTexts.Set("Win", "哦~，老夫终于赢了一次，人类终于赢了一次！");

        self._locale.Set("English", englishTexts);
        self._locale.Set("简体中文", chineseTexts);

        self._profiles.Add(Profile("Armin", "Armin1"));
        self._profiles.Add(Profile("Jean", "Jean1"));
        self._profiles.Add(Profile("Pixis", "Pixis1"));
    }

    function ShowDialogue(key, profileIndex, delay)
    {
        NetworkMessage()
            .Set("Type", "Dialogue")
            .Set("Key", key)
            .Set("ProfileIndex", profileIndex)
            .Set("Delay", delay)
            .SendAll();
    }

    coroutine _ShowDialogueDelayed(key, profileIndex, delay)
    {
        if (delay != null && delay > 0)
        {
            wait delay;
        }

        self._ShowDialogue(key, profileIndex);
    }

    coroutine _ShowDialogue(key, profileIndex)
    {
        lang = Locale.CurrentLanguage;
        if (!self._locale.Contains(lang))
        {
            lang = "English";
        }

        text = self._locale.Get(lang).Get(key);
        profile = self._profiles.Get(profileIndex);
        title = self._locale.Get(lang).Get(profile.Name);
        Cutscene.ShowDialogue(profile.Icon, title, text);
        wait 4.0;
        Cutscene.HideDialogue();
    }
}

class Profile
{
    Name = "Eren";
    Icon = "Eren1";

    function Init(name, icon)
    {
        self.Name = name;
        self.Icon = icon;
    }
}
extension InGameUI
{
    function UpdateRoundTime(totalSeconds)
    {
        minutes = totalSeconds / 60;
        seconds = Math.Mod(totalSeconds, 60);

        formattedMinutes = Convert.ToString(minutes);
        formattedSeconds = Convert.ToString(seconds);

        if (minutes < 10)
        {
            formattedMinutes = "0" + minutes;
        }

        if (seconds < 10)
        {
            formattedSeconds = "0" + seconds;
        }

        formattedTime = formattedMinutes + ":" + formattedSeconds;

        UI.SetLabelAll("TopLeft", formattedTime);
    }
}
extension CaptureZones
{
    _captureZones = null;

    /* 
     * Some empty map objects around the HQ.
     * Titans will target one of these instead of the HQ itself
     * for pathfinding reasons.
     */
    _titanTargets = null;

    HeadquarterZone = null;

    function Setup(main)
    {
        self._captureZones = List();
        captureZoneOrderMap = Dict();
        for(z in Map.FindMapObjectsByName("CaptureZone1"))
        {
            c = z.GetComponent("CaptureZone");
            c.SetupCallbackReceiver(main);
            if (captureZoneOrderMap.Contains(c.Order) == true)
            {
                Game.Print("Capture zone order " + c.Order + " is already added, please remove duplicate zone!");
                Game.End(10);
                return;
            }
            captureZoneOrderMap.Set(c.Order, c);
        }

        keys = captureZoneOrderMap.Keys;
        keys.Sort();
        for(key in keys)
        {
            self._captureZones.Add(captureZoneOrderMap.Get(key));
        }

        self._titanTargets = Map.FindMapObjectsByTag("TitanTarget");

        self.HeadquarterZone = Map.FindMapObjectByTag("CaptureZoneHeadquarter").GetComponent("CaptureZone");
        self.HeadquarterZone.SetupCallbackReceiver(main);
    }

    function SetActiveCaptureZones(active)
    {
        self.HeadquarterZone.Enabled = active;
        self.HeadquarterZone.MapObject.Active = active;

        for(cz in self._captureZones)
        {
            cz.MapObject.Active = active;
        }
    }

    function Count()
    {
        return self._captureZones.Count;
    }

    function AreZonesCapturedByHumans()
    {
        return self.HumanZones().Count == self.Count();
    }

    function GetTitanSpawnPoint()
    {
        zone = null;
        nonTitanZones = self.NonTitanZones();
        if (nonTitanZones.Count == 0)
        {
            zone = Utils.GetRandomListElement(self._captureZones)/* .MapObject.Position */;
        }
        else
        {
            randomNonTitanZone = Utils.GetRandomListElement(nonTitanZones);
            zone = self._NearestZone(randomNonTitanZone.MapObject.Position, self.TitanZones())/* .MapObject.Position */;
        }

        return TitanSpawnPoints.GetSpawnPoint(zone);
    }

    function GetTitanTarget(position)
    {
        nonTitanZones = self.NonTitanZones();
        if (nonTitanZones.Count == 0)
        {
            return self._NearestTitanTarget(position).Position;
        }

        attackHq = 0.7;
        attackZone = 0.3;

        nearest = self.NearestNonTitanZone(position);
        distToZone = Vector3.Distance(position, nearest.MapObject.Position);
        distToHq = Vector3.Distance(position, self.HeadquarterZone.MapObject.Position);

        if (distToZone < distToHq)
        {
            attackHq = 0.35;
            attackZone = 0.65;
        }

        r = Random.RandomFloat(0, 1);
        if (r <= attackHq && r > attackZone)
        {
            return self._NearestTitanTarget(position).Position;
        }
        elif (r <= attackZone)
        {
            return nearest.MapObject.Position;
        }
        
        return self._NearestTitanTarget(position).Position;
    }

    function NearestNonTitanZone(position)
    {
        return self._NearestZone(position, self.NonTitanZones());
    }

    function TitanZones()
    {
        return self._ZonesOfTeam("Titan", false);
    }

    function NonTitanZones()
    {
        return self._ZonesOfTeam("Titan", true);
    }

    function HumanZones()
    {
        return self._ZonesOfTeam("Human", false);
    }

    function _ZonesOfTeam(team, not)
    {
        zones = List();
        for(z in self._captureZones)
        {
            if (not)
            {
                if (z.GetCurrentOwner() != team)
                {
                    zones.Add(z);
                }
            }
            else
            {
                if (z.GetCurrentOwner() == team)
                {
                    zones.Add(z);
                }
            }
        }
        return zones;
    }

    function _NearestZone(position, zones)
    {
        zone = null;
        dist = Math.Infinity;

        for(z in zones)
        {
            p = z.MapObject.Position;
            d = Vector3.Distance(position, p);
            if (d < dist)
            {
                zone = z;
                dist = d;
            }
        }

        return zone;
    }

    function _NearestTitanTarget(position)
    {
        out = null;
        dist = Math.Infinity;

        for(t in self._titanTargets)
        {
            p = t.Position;
            d = Vector3.Distance(position, p);
            if (d < dist)
            {
                out = t;
                dist = d;
            }
        }

        return out;
    }
}
extension Titans
{
    MaxTitans = 30;
    MinSpawnInterval = 10.0;
    MaxSpawnInterval = 30.0;

    _spawning = false;
    _nextSpawnTime = 0.0;

    _titans = List();
    _headquarterTitans = List();

    function Setup(maxTitans, spawnRatePercentage)
    {
        self.MaxTitans = Math.Max(10, maxTitans);

        t = Math.Clamp(Convert.ToFloat(spawnRatePercentage), 0.0, 100.0) / 100.0;
        self.MinSpawnInterval = Math.Lerp(1, 13, 1.0 - t);
        self.MaxSpawnInterval = Math.Lerp(5, 26, 1.0 - t);
    }

    function SpawnHeadquarterTitans()
    {
        spawnPoints = Map.FindMapObjectsByTag("TitanSpawnPointHeadquarter");
        for(sp in spawnPoints)
        {
            titan = Game.SpawnTitanAt("Normal", sp.Position);
            titan.Size = Random.RandomFloat(0.5, 1);
            titan.UsePathfinding = false;
            titan.Position = sp.Position;
            self._headquarterTitans.Add(titan);
        }
    }

    function StartSpawn()
    {
        if (self._spawning)
        {
            return;
        }

        self._spawning = true;
        self._nextSpawnTime = self._GetSpawnInterval();
    }

    function Update()
    {
        if (GameState.Ended)
        {
            return;
        }
        
        if (!self._spawning || self._titans.Count > self.MaxTitans)
        {
            return;
        }

        if (Time.GameTime >= self._nextSpawnTime)
        {
            pos = CaptureZones.GetTitanSpawnPoint() + Vector3(0, 10, 0);
            target = CaptureZones.GetTitanTarget(pos);
            if (target != null)
            {
                titan = Game.SpawnTitanAt("Default", pos);
                titan.MoveTo(target, 1, false);
                titan.DetectRange = 70;
                titan.FocusRange = 70;

                self._titans.Add(titan);
            }
            self._nextSpawnTime = Time.GameTime + self._GetSpawnInterval();
        }
    }

    function RemoveTitan(titan)
    {
        if (!GameState.DefendStarted && Utils.TryRemoveListElement(self._headquarterTitans, titan))
        {
            if (self._headquarterTitans.Count == 0)
            {
                GameState.StartDefendPhase();
            }
        }

        if (Utils.TryRemoveListElement(self._titans, titan) && self.CheckForWin())
        {
            GameState.End(true);
        }
    }

    function CheckForWin()
    {
        return CaptureZones.AreZonesCapturedByHumans() && self._titans.Count == 0;
    }

    function _GetSpawnInterval()
    {
        total = CaptureZones.Count();
        titans = CaptureZones.TitanZones().Count;
        t = Math.Lerp(self.MaxSpawnInterval, self.MinSpawnInterval, Convert.ToFloat(titans) / Convert.ToFloat(total));
        return t;
    }
}
extension SupplyAndTpZones
{
    function Setup()
    {
        self._supplyStations = List();
        self._teleportZone = Map.FindMapObjectByTag("HqTpZone").GetComponent("TeleportRegion");
        for(ss in Map.FindMapObjectsByTag("HqStation"))
        {
            self._supplyStations.Add(ss.GetComponent("SupplyStation"));
        }
    }

    function SetEnabled(enabled)
    {
        self._teleportZone.TeleportHumans = enabled;
        for(ss in self._supplyStations)
        {
            ss.UnlimitedRefills = enabled;
        }
    }
}
extension TitanSpawnPoints
{
    _spawnPoints = Dict();

    function Setup()
    {
        spawnPoints = Map.FindMapObjectsByTag("TitanSpawnPoint");
        for(sp in spawnPoints)
        {
            zone = CaptureZones._NearestZone(sp.Position, CaptureZones._captureZones);
            self._spawnPoints.Set(zone, sp);
        }
    }

    function GetSpawnPoint(zone)
    {
        if (self._spawnPoints.Contains(zone))
        {
            return self._spawnPoints.Get(zone).Position;
        }

        return zone.MapObject.Position;
    }
}
class NetworkMessage
{
    Params = Dict();

    function Set(name, value)
    {
        self.Params.Set(name, value);
        return self;
    }

    function SendAll()
    {
        Network.SendMessageAll(self.ToString());
    }

    function SendOthers()
    {
        Network.SendMessageOthers(self.ToString());
    }

    function Send(player)
    {
        Network.SendMessage(player, self.ToString());
    }

    function ToString()
    {
        return Json.SaveToString(self.Params);
    }
}
extension Utils
{
    function GetRandomListElement(list)
    {
        i = Random.RandomInt(0, list.Count);
        return list.Get(i);
    }

    function IndexOfListElement(list, element)
    {
        i = 0;
        while (i < list.Count)
        {
            if (list.Get(i) == element)
            {
                return i;
            }

            i += 1;
        }

        return -1;
    }

    function TryRemoveListElement(list, element)
    {
        index = self.IndexOfListElement(list, element);
        if (index != -1)
        {
            list.RemoveAt(index);
            return true;
        }

        return false;
    }

    function ListContains(list, element)
    {
        return self.IndexOfListElement(list, element) >= 0;
    }
}
